          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





1.tar -zxvf a.tar.gz -C /tmp



<span class="line"><!---->1.tar -zxvf a.tar.gz -C /tmp<!----></span>



<br>





2.out/asan/chrome --load-extension=/tmp/poc_extension1/media-gallery,/tmp/poc_extension1/embeded_host  --user-data-dir=/tmp/bfdab



<span class="line"><!---->2.out/asan/chrome --load-extension=/tmp/poc_extension1/media-gallery,/tmp/poc_extension1/embeded_host  --user-data-dir=/tmp/bfdab<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





There is only a DCHECK in [1] to check the needed rph is in observer_map_. 



<span class="line"><!---->There is only a DCHECK in [1] to check the needed rph is in observer_map_. <!----></span>



<br>





However If webcontents navigated twice then RPHReferenceManager::OnWebContentsDestroyedOrNavigate will be called twice.



<span class="line"><!---->However If webcontents navigated twice then RPHReferenceManager::OnWebContentsDestroyedOrNavigate will be called twice.<!----></span>



<br>





At the first call rph_info will be removed from the observer_map_ in [2]. So in the second call rph_info == observer_map_.end lead to heap buffer overflow when accessing rph_info in [3].



<span class="line"><!---->At the first call rph_info will be removed from the observer_map_ in [2]. So in the second call rph_info == observer_map_.end lead to heap buffer overflow when accessing rph_info in [3].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





void RPHReferenceManager::OnRenderProcessHostDestroyed(



<span class="line"><!---->void RPHReferenceManager::OnRenderProcessHostDestroyed(<!----></span>



<br>





    RenderProcessHost* rph) {



<span class="line"><!---->    RenderProcessHost* rph) {<!----></span>



<br>





  auto rph_info = observer_map_.find(rph);



<span class="line"><!---->  auto rph_info = observer_map_.find(rph);<!----></span>



<br>





  // This could be a potential problem if the RPH is navigated to a page on the



<span class="line"><!---->  // This could be a potential problem if the RPH is navigated to a page on the<!----></span>



<br>





  // same renderer (triggering OnWebContentsDestroyedOrNavigated()) and then the



<span class="line"><!---->  // same renderer (triggering OnWebContentsDestroyedOrNavigated()) and then the<!----></span>



<br>





  // renderer crashes.



<span class="line"><!---->  // renderer crashes.<!----></span>



<br>





  if (rph_info == observer_map_.end()) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (rph_info == observer_map_.end()) {<!----></span>



<br>





    NOTREACHED();



<span class="line"><!---->    NOTREACHED();<!----></span>



<br>





    return;



<span class="line"><!---->    return;<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





  observer_map_.erase(rph_info);   -----------[2]



<span class="line"><!---->  observer_map_.erase(rph_info);   -----------[2]<!----></span>



<br>





  if (observer_map_.empty())



<span class="line"><!---->  if (observer_map_.empty())<!----></span>



<br>





    std::move(no_references_callback_).Run();



<span class="line"><!---->    std::move(no_references_callback_).Run();<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





void RPHReferenceManager::OnWebContentsDestroyedOrNavigated(



<span class="line"><!---->void RPHReferenceManager::OnWebContentsDestroyedOrNavigated(<!----></span>



<br>





    WebContents* contents) {



<span class="line"><!---->    WebContents* contents) {<!----></span>



<br>





  RenderProcessHost* rph = contents->GetPrimaryMainFrame()->GetProcess();



<span class="line"><!---->  RenderProcessHost* rph = contents-&gt;GetPrimaryMainFrame()-&gt;GetProcess();<!----></span>



<br>





  auto rph_info = observer_map_.find(rph);



<span class="line"><!---->  auto rph_info = observer_map_.find(rph);<!----></span>



<br>





  DCHECK(rph_info != observer_map_.end());   -------------[1]



<span class="line"><!---->  DCHECK(rph_info != observer_map_.end());   -------------[1]<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  rph_info->second->RemoveWebContentsObserver(contents);---------[3]



<span class="line"><!---->  rph_info-&gt;second-&gt;RemoveWebContentsObserver(contents);---------[3]<!----></span>



<br>





  if (!rph_info->second->HasWebContentsObservers())



<span class="line"><!---->  if (!rph_info-&gt;second-&gt;HasWebContentsObservers())<!----></span>



<br>





    OnRenderProcessHostDestroyed(rph);



<span class="line"><!---->    OnRenderProcessHostDestroyed(rph);<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





}  // namespace



<span class="line"><!---->}  // namespace<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

I was able to repro. I added some logging, and there's only one insertion and one lookup.



<span class="line"><!---->I was able to repro. I added some logging, and there's only one insertion and one lookup.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I think the problem is that the insertion takes place using the RenderProcessHost of the old RFH before navigation, but the second lookup happens *after* the navigation.



<span class="line"><!---->I think the problem is that the insertion takes place using the RenderProcessHost of the old RFH before navigation, but the second lookup happens *after* the navigation.<!----></span>



<br>

Hello Lei/DCheng,



<span class="line"><!---->Hello Lei/DCheng,<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I've been investigating this code this morning, and it seems like ExtensionGalleriesHost was at one point meant to be shared between multiple tabs, likely as an optimization to allow sharing of the internal state.



<span class="line"><!---->I've been investigating this code this morning, and it seems like ExtensionGalleriesHost was at one point meant to be shared between multiple tabs, likely as an optimization to allow sharing of the internal state.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Do we typically have multiple tabs all using Media Galleries? If not, I'd like to suggest a radical simplification (as dcheng suggested in c#5) of making ExtensionGalleriesHost a PageUserData rather than refcounted.



<span class="line"><!---->Do we typically have multiple tabs all using Media Galleries? If not, I'd like to suggest a radical simplification (as dcheng suggested in c#5) of making ExtensionGalleriesHost a PageUserData rather than refcounted.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The registry class can still keep around a non-owning WeakPtr to do bookkeeping, but we get rid of the RPHReferenceManager entirely.



<span class="line"><!---->The registry class can still keep around a non-owning WeakPtr to do bookkeeping, but we get rid of the RPHReferenceManager entirely.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Thanks,



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks,<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tommy



<span class="line"><!---->Tommy<!----></span>

The following revision refers to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->The following revision refers to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>





  



<span class="line"><!---->  <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/9e66dcab109672defbf0d81fb02bb71b786b0ce3



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/9e66dcab109672defbf0d81fb02bb71b786b0ce3"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/9e66dcab109672defbf0d81fb02bb71b786b0ce3<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





9e66dcab109672defbf0d81fb02bb71b786b0ce3



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/9e66dcab109672defbf0d81fb02bb71b786b0ce3"><!---->9e66dcab109672defbf0d81fb02bb71b786b0ce3<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Tommy C. Li <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Tommy C. Li &lt;<!----></span>





tommycli@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/tommycli@chromium.org"><!---->tommycli@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Tue Aug 23 22:33:54 2022



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Tue Aug 23 22:33:54 2022<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[media_galleries] Fix crash and simplify MediaFileSystemRegistry



<span class="line"><!---->[media_galleries] Fix crash and simplify MediaFileSystemRegistry<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





ExtensionGalleriesHost has a complicated lifetime. It was originally



<span class="line"><!---->ExtensionGalleriesHost has a complicated lifetime. It was originally<!----></span>



<br>





intended to be scoped to the lifetime of every tab that called a



<span class="line"><!---->intended to be scoped to the lifetime of every tab that called a<!----></span>



<br>





particular combination of Profile and extension_id.



<span class="line"><!---->particular combination of Profile and extension_id.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





It used a bespoke system called RPHReferenceManager to manage this, but



<span class="line"><!---->It used a bespoke system called RPHReferenceManager to manage this, but<!----></span>



<br>





unfortunately, it likely broke due to either site-per-process or MPArch.



<span class="line"><!---->unfortunately, it likely broke due to either site-per-process or MPArch.<!----></span>



<br>





I'm not sure what caused the breakage, but in any case, there's memory



<span class="line"><!---->I'm not sure what caused the breakage, but in any case, there's memory<!----></span>



<br>





issues as documented in the bug.



<span class="line"><!---->issues as documented in the bug.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This CL tries redo it using PageUserData, and scope the lifetime to the



<span class="line"><!---->This CL tries redo it using PageUserData, and scope the lifetime to the<!----></span>



<br>





lives of all the content::Page instances that refer to this combo of



<span class="line"><!---->lives of all the content::Page instances that refer to this combo of<!----></span>



<br>





Profile and extension_id.



<span class="line"><!---->Profile and extension_id.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





It also changes it from ref-counted to a unique-pointer. This simplifies



<span class="line"><!---->It also changes it from ref-counted to a unique-pointer. This simplifies<!----></span>



<br>





the lifetime semantics a bit further.



<span class="line"><!---->the lifetime semantics a bit further.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Bug: 1343384



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1343384" title="heap-buffer-overflow in RPHReferenceManager::OnWebContentsDestroyedOrNavigated"><!---->Bug: 1343384<!----></a>



<br>





Change-Id: I293c3e6af5e38b8fe47cc8c1991dac17ef6fc3da



<span class="line"><!---->Change-Id: I293c3e6af5e38b8fe47cc8c1991dac17ef6fc3da<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward.
